-- OLD Decision

WITH 
MEMBER [Measures].[Number of Facilities - Ratio] AS
'([Measures].[Number of Facilities], [Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].CurrentMember) / ([Measures].[Number of Facilities]
, {[Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].CurrentMember.Parent, [Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].CurrentMember}.Item(0))', SOLVE_ORDER = 25

MEMBER [Measures].[Facility Exposure, End - Ratio] AS
'([Measures].[Facility Exposure, End], [Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].CurrentMember) / ([Measures].[Facility Exposure, End]
, {[Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].CurrentMember.Parent, [Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].CurrentMember}.Item(0))', SOLVE_ORDER = 26

MEMBER [Measures].[Facility Exposure, Average - Ratio] AS
'([Measures].[Facility Exposure, Average], [Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].CurrentMember) / ([Measures].[Facility Exposure, Average]
, {[Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].CurrentMember.Parent, [Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].CurrentMember}.Item(0))', SOLVE_ORDER = 27

MEMBER [Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].[Blah] AS
'[Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].[All RRR] / [Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].[RR2K].&[125]', SOLVE_ORDER = 28

SELECT 
{
DISTINCT({({[Measures].[Facility Exposure, End]})
      , ({[Measures].[Facility Exposure, End - Ratio]})
	  , ({[Measures].[Facility Exposure, Average]})
	  , ({[Measures].[Facility Exposure, Average - Ratio]})
	  , ({[Measures].[Number of Facilities]})
	  , ({[Measures].[Number of Facilities - Ratio]})})
	  } DIMENSION PROPERTIES MEMBER_NAME, PARENT_UNIQUE_NAME, IS_DATAMEMBER ON COLUMNS, 
NON EMPTY {
          DISTINCT({
		          ({[Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].[All RRR]})
		        , ({[Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].[Blah]})
		        , ({[Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].[RR2K].&[115]})
		        , ({[Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].[RR2K].&[116]})
		        , ({[Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].[RR2K].&[117]})
		        , ({[Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].[RR2K].&[118]})
		        , ({[Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].[RR2K].&[119]})
		        , ({[Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].[RR2K].&[120]})
		        , ({[Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].[RR2K].&[121]})
		        , ({[Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].[RR2K].&[122]})
		        , ({[Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].[RR2K].&[123]})
		        , ({[Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].[RR2K].&[124]})
		        , ({[Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].[RR2K].&[125]})
		        , ({[Obligor Risk Rating].[RRR Hierarchy].[RR2K].&[199]})}
				)} DIMENSION PROPERTIES MEMBER_NAME, PARENT_UNIQUE_NAME, IS_DATAMEMBER ON ROWS
FROM [LW Cube]
WHERE ([Accruing Status].[Accrual Status].[All Accrual Status], [Bank Owned Managed].[Bank Owned Managed].[All Bank Owned], [Collateral].[Collateral Hierarchy].[All Collateral], [Currency Type].[Currency Type].[Organization in USD $], [Customer Geography].[Geography By Region].[All Geography By Region], [Days Past Due].[Past Due Days].[All Past Due Days], [Deal Size].[Deal Size].[All Deal Sizes], [Exception Type].[Exception Types].[All Exception Types], [Fed Class Code].[FCC].[All Fed Class Code], [Fee Type].[Fee Type Hierarchy].[All Fee Type], [IFRS].[Risk Rating Key].[All LQC (IFRS)], [Industry NAIC Code].[NAICS].[All Industries by NAICS], [Lending Entity].[Lending Entity].[All Lending Entity], [Obligation Risk Rating].[LQC_GAAP Hierarchy].[All LQC/GAAP], [Obligation Type].[Obligation Type].[All Types], [Org by Bank Obligor].[Parent].[All Customers & Obligations], [Org by Group].[Org  by Group].[All Groups], [Organization].[Hierarchy].[All Rabo], [Pricing Index].[Interest Base].[All Interest Bases], [Process Type].[PT Hierarchy].[All Process Type], [Product].[Product Hierarchy].[All Product], [TDR].[TDR Hierarchy].[All TDR], [Time].[Monthly].[All Time by Month].[Current Month], [Upcoming Maturity].[Upcoming Maturity].[All Upcoming Maturity], [Vintage].[Vintage Absolute].[All Vintage])
